border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(0, 0, 0);font-size: 14px;font-family: Optima-Regular, PingFangTC-light;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">早读|口语|阅读|翻译|听写</p><p style="text-align: left;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">编辑|排版 Claire</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(62, 62, 62);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">circumstance </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈsɜːkəmstəns  ;英 ˈsɜːkəmstɑːns  ; 美 ˈsɜːkəmstæns /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 环境, 条件, 情况，境遇, 经济状况</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's a little awkward under the circumstances.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在的情况有点尴尬。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Firing somebody is hard under any circumstances.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">无论如何，解雇某人是一件很困难的事。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">automatically</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˌɔ:tə'mætikəli/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adv. 自动地，无意识地,不自觉地,机械地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">automatic / ˌɔːtəˈmætɪk /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 自动的,不假思索的, 无意识的,必然发生的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 能自动运转的机器或器械</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">And he seemed nice, you know? We seemed to automatically connect.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他人好像不错 你知道吗? 我们自然而然的走到一起。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">As soon as I touch someone's hair, I start braiding automatically.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">当我的手碰到别人的头发，就忍不住给他们编辫子。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> in order to  为了</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Understand yourself in order to better understand others.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">了解自己以便更好的了解别人。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reset the lungs 重置肺部活动</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reset / ˌriːˈset/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 重新安放或安置,重拨(测量仪器指针),为(考试、测试等)出一套新题</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to reset a broken bone 重接断骨</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You need to reset your watch to local time. 你需要把表调整到当地时间。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Now for me, the ultimate way of resetting is to go outside.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对我而言，最直接的恢复办法就是出去走走。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lung</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/lʌŋ/ n. 肺；呼吸器 </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lung cancer肺癌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">setting</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/'setɪŋ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 环境；布置；安装；沉落</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v. 放置；沉没；使…处于某位置（set的ing形式）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">set/set/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 集合；一套；布景；装置；趋势</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 树立；点燃；放；点缀；使凝结</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 凝固；结果；定型</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 固定的；规定的；固执的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">verb</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/vɜ:b/n. 动词；动词词性；动词性短语或从句</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj. 动词的；有动词性质的；起动词作用的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> regular/irregular verbs 规则╱不规则动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> transitive/intransitive verbs 及物╱不及物动词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">noun / naʊn / n.名词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adjective / ˈædʒɪktɪv/ n.形容词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adverb / ˈædvɜːb/ n.副词</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Adverbs are used to modify verbs and adjectives.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">副词用来修饰动词和形容词。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Content words are nouns, verbs, adjectives, and adverbs.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">实词是名词，动词，形容词，还有副词。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">UCLA </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">University of California at Los Angeles </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">加利福尼亚大学洛杉矶分校</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Los Angeles洛杉矶</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">breath</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/breθ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 气息; 呼吸,(一次)呼吸, 一口气; 微风</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We were scant of breath after the lengthy climb.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">长时间的运动后，我们感觉呼吸困难。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How long can you hold your breath?</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你能憋气多久？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">breathe/bri:ð/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 呼吸；低语；松口气；（风）轻拂</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 呼吸；流露；使喘息；低声说</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He came up close, breathing alcohol fumes all over me. 他走过来靠近我，喷得我满身酒气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">sac</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/sæk/ n. [生物]液囊；囊</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Your lungs are like sponges that are made of tiny air sacs.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你的肺脏就像海绵，由许多小小气囊组成。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">alveoli/ æl'viəlai/ n.气泡,肺泡类；齿槽突起</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Alveoli dentales 齿槽</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Working properly 工作正常</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">properly / ˈprɒpəli/ adv. 适当地；正确地；恰当地</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The car has always been properly maintained.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这汽车一直保养得很好。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">collapse </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ kəˈlæps/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vi. 倒塌；瓦解；暴跌</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">vt. 使倒塌，使崩溃；使萎陷</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n. 倒塌；失败；衰竭</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Until one day, I collapsed with exhaustion.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">直到有一天，我累倒了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The gypsum mine collapsed on Christmas Day.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">圣诞节当天，该石膏矿发生坍塌。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">oxygen </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈɒksɪdʒən / n.氧气，氧</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Water is composed of hydrogen and oxygen.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">水是由氢和氧组成的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Deprived of oxygen, the bird begins to suffocate.</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">失去了氧气 鸟开始窒息。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读</span></span></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: So sighing keep<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s us a</span></span>live.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">所以叹气能让我们活着。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Dr Barker calle<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d it a</span></span> survival mechanism. To survive means to continue living, especially in difficul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> circumstances. A mechanism, here, means a system of behaviour.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">贝克博士把叹气叫作生存机制。生存就是继续活着，尤其是在艰难的环境中。机制是指一种行为系统。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: So, a survival mechanism is something the body does automatically in order to survive. But, Dan, why is sighing a survival mechanism?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">生存机制是指身体为了生存而自动做出的反应。但是，丹，为什么叹气是一种生存机制呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: It's because sighing can reset the lungs. To reset is to return something t<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">o its o</span></span>riginal settings. W<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e o</span></span>ften use this verb when talki<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng a</span></span>bout technology. You can rese<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a </span></span>computer o<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">r a</span></span> phone.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">因为叹气能重置肺部活动。重置是指让某物恢复到原始的设置状态。谈论科技时，我们经常会用到这个词。你可以重置电脑或手机。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: OK, that's fine. Bu<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> how doe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> sigh reset the lungs?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">很好。那叹气是如何重置肺部活动呢？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Well, scientists from UCLA, that's the Universit<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y o</span></span>f California, Lo<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s A</span></span>ngeles, found tha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span> sigh i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> special kin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d o</span></span>f very deep breath tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> keeps the tiny sacs of air i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n o</span></span>ur lungs, called alveoli, working properly.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">加州大学洛杉矶分校（</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">UCLA</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">）的科学家们发现，叹气是一种特殊的深呼吸，能让我们肺部中微小的空气囊</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">——</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">肺泡合理运转。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: An<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> without sighing, these alveoli woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>collapse an<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>we woul<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> die. We nee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d </span></span>the alveoli to transfer oxygen fro<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">m o</span></span>ur lungs to our blood.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没有叹气，这些肺泡就会破裂，我们就会死亡。我们需要用肺泡把肺中的氧气送至血液。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Can you imagine a stretch of grassy land bubbling like water in a pot? For that is really the best description of what was happening. In all directions it was swelling into humps. They were of very different sizes, some no bigger than mole-hills, some as big as wheel-barrows, two the size of cottages. And the humps moved and swelled till they burst, and the crumbled earth poured out of them, and from each hump there came out an animal.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你能想像一块草地像壶里的水一样沸腾吗，但这样描述正存发生的事是最最恰当的。周围的草地膨胀成个个大小不同的圆丘，有的只有鼹鼠丘那么大，有的和独轮小车相差无几，其中两个与小棚屋一般大小。这些圆丘移动着，膨胀着，直到泥土四溅地炸开后，每个圆丘里都钻出一样动物。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你好，我能换一些钱吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 我们手头没有那么多现金。您能今天少换一点儿，明天再来换余下的部分吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好吧，今天最多能换多少？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 换200美元够用吗？我们一次最多能兑换200美元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 好吧，我想只能这样了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Hello. Can I change some money, please?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: I'm afraid we don't have that much cash on hand. Could you change a little less today, then come back tomorrow to change the rest?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Okay. What's the most I can change today?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Would $200 be enough? The most we can change at one time is $200.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Well, I suppose it will have to do.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Such a plan, in my opinion, is ____________ impractical.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">照我看来，这样一个计划无疑是行不通的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">without a doubt</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">仅仅有人在身旁并不能起到治疗的作用。对人们来说，仅仅感到被孤立就足以产生对健康不利的影响。尽管孤独感有如此重大的影响 ，但是它是如何在人群中传播的——却不为人知。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Simply being surrounded by others is no cure. In people, the mere perception of being isolated is more than enough to create the bad health effects. However, in spite of its significant impact, precious little is known about how loneliness moves through communities.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>9.28 每日一句：</strong><strong><span style="text-align: justify;">Silver lining.      </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong>不幸中的万幸<span lang="EN-US">/</span>（困境中的）一线希望</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong><span style="text-align: justify;"></span></strong></p><section style="box-sizing: border-box;">You can balloon up or you can shrink down and I'll still love you.</span></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>1. ba</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>lloon</strong></span><strong> /bəˈluːn/ 注意元音/u:/到鼻音/n/的过渡，不要读成“路温”；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>2. </strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>shr</strong></span><strong>ink /ʃrɪŋk/ 注意单词内部辅音连缀；</strong></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong>3. I'</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>ll</strong></span><strong> sti</strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong>ll</strong></span><strong> 两个单词尾部都包含舌侧音/l/。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. balloon</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ noun. 气球</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to blow up/burst/pop a balloon</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">吹起气球；吹爆气球</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">blew up a balloon</span></em></strong> but then it burst.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吹了一个气球</strong>，但后来它爆了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.25" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKeQjCxxht7GL3uMrbBgDCS3MibBJ1Cfu914o3wYuibgCODNzbbZMpjH57DLk37AiboQRIH4Pveianxutw/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→ verb. 膨胀，鼓起来；突然长胖</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Paul <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ballooned</span></em></strong> after he got married.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">保罗婚后<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">吹气球似地胖了起来</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ballooned</span></em></strong> when I became pregnant with my second baby.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">怀第二个孩子时，我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">胖得像个气球</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链儿：balloon out/up 突然膨胀，涨大</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Her skirt <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">ballooned out/up</span></em></strong> in the wind.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她的裙子让风吹得<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">鼓起来</strong>了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>...causing her to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">balloon up</span></em></strong> to gain hundreds of pounds.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">导致她的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">体重暴增</strong>数百磅。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>All of those can lead your legs to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">balloon up</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">所有这些都会导致你的腿<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">膨胀</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. shrink 与 balloon 含义相反</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→verb. 使缩小，使收缩</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We want to expand the business, not <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">shrink</span></em></strong> it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们要扩大业务，而不是<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">缩小</strong>。 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My sweater <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">shrank</span></em></strong> in the wash.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我的毛衣<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">缩水</strong>了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reset /ˌriːˈset/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">to change a clock, control, machine etc so that it shows a different time or number, or is ready to be used again v.重新设置；调整；重新安置；将…恢复原位</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lung /lʌŋ/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">reflex  /ˈriːfleks/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.反射的；反作用的(效果,音响等)；反省的；回想的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.反射动作；本能反应；反射作用</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">knee jerk reflex 膝跳反射</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">blink reflex 眨眼反射</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">fabulous  /ˈfæbjələs/   </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">extremely good or impressive adj.极好的；绝妙的；</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You look fabulous!你看起来棒极了！</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">very large in amount or size adj.很大的；巨大的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">the Duke’s fabulous wealth 公爵令人难以置信的财富</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">meant /ment/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">mean/miːn/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">To breathe a sigh of relief 如释重负</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">relieved /rɪˈliːvd/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">feeling happy because you are no longer worried about something adj.感到宽慰的；放心的；显得开心的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She looked immensely relieved when she heard the news.听到这个消息时，她看起来松了一口气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">metaphorical  /ˌmetəˈfɒrɪkəl◂ $ -ˈfɔː-, -ˈfɑː-/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a metaphorical use of a word is not concerned with real objects or physical events, but with ideas or events of a non-physical kind adj.隐喻性的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The word has a metaphorical as well as a literal meaning.这个词既有比喻的意思，也有字面上的意思。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">relate  /rɪˈleɪt/  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">if two things relate, they are connected in some way v.联系；讲述；叙述；使有联系</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I don’t understand how the two ideas relate.我不明白这两个想法有什么关系。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">frustration /frʌˈstreɪʃən/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">he feeling of being annoyed, upset, or impatient, because you cannot control or change a situation, or achieve something .n.沮丧；受挫；挫败；懊丧</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">People often feel a sense of frustration that they are not being promoted quickly enough.人们经常感到非常沮丧，因为他们升职的速度不够快。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">frustrating  /frʌˈstreɪtɪŋ $ ˈfrʌstreɪtɪŋ/ </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">making you feel annoyed, upset, or impatient because you cannot do what you want to do adj.令人懊恼的；令人沮丧的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My job can be very frustrating sometimes.我的工作有时非常令人沮丧。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">resignation /ˌrezɪɡˈneɪʃən/</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">an occasion when you officially announce that you have decided to leave your job or an organization, or a written statement that says you will be leaving n.辞职；辞呈；顺从；辞职信</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Illness forced his resignation.疾病迫使他辞职。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> when someone calmly accepts a situation that cannot be changed, even though it is bad 无可奈何</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She gave a sigh of resignation.她无奈地叹了口气。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section 0px 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="padding-bottom: 8px;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="clear: none;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">听写方法：</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">完成今天的任务了么？不！千万不要丢掉极其重要的一步：校对！</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">有两个方面要校对：</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.没有听出来的意群：可能包括连读或者省音,分析错误的原因并做笔记。</p><p style="color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.94);font-size: 12px;white-space: normal;caret-color: rgb(81, 81, 81);clear: none;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.没有听出来或听错的单词:每篇校对后写在听写笔记下面并罗列,这些才是你每天的进步之基。</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(188, 132, 37);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">今日听写答案</p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: center;color: rgba(122, 120, 124, 0.91);font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">（请务必听写后校对） </span></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;">红色连读</span><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">；<span style="color: rgba(46, 159, 238, 0.863);box-sizing: border-box;">蓝色爆破省读</span>；<span style="color: rgb(255, 129, 36);box-sizing: border-box;">橙色弱读 <span style="font-size: 14px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></span></span></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">Wednesday</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Thankfully, we don't have to thin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k a</span></span>bout this nee<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">reset </strong>our <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">lungs</strong>. Sighing i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s i</span></span>n fact a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">reflex</strong>.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">幸好我们不用专门想着重置肺部活动。叹气实际上是一种本能反应。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Boo!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">砰！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Argh!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">哎呀！</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: There – you jumped! And tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> wa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">fabulous </strong>reflex, Dan! It's something our bodies do withou<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> thinking, something you d<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">o u</span></span>nconsciously or automatically.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你都跳起来了！这就是不可思议的本能反应。本能反应是指未经大脑思考，身体做出的反应，也就是说你无意识地做了某事。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: I meant… argh… li<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ke a</span></span> man. Thank you for that, Catherine.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我是说你的反应很正常。谢谢你啊，凯瑟琳。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: You're welcome.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">不客气。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: Do you sigh a lot?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你经常叹气吗？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Well, I sigh whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span>'m tired, an<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d I</span></span> sigh whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span>'m <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">relieved</strong>. I breathe a sigh of relief.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">我累的时候会叹气，解脱的时候也会叹气。如释重负。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">To breathe a s<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">igh o</span></span>f relief</strong> – that'<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s a</span></span> great expression. It means wha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> you thin<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">k i</span></span>t means – to sigh when you feel good tha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> something bad has no<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> happened– but i<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t's o</span></span>ften used <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">metaphorically</strong>. It <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">relates </strong>more to the feeli<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng o</span></span>f relief than the ac<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t o</span></span>f sighing.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">如释重负，也是一个不错的表达。坏事未发生，感觉不错时，你会叹气。通常用作隐喻。更多的是体现一种放松的感觉，而不是叹气的动作。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: That's right. Now, I breathed a si<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">gh o</span></span>f relief whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span> found my mobile phone th<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">e o</span></span>ther day. I thought I'd los<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t i</span></span>t. I<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> was new. I wa<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s s</span></span>o pleased whe<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">n I</span></span> foun<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">d i</span></span>t! Wha<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">t a</span></span>bout you, Dan?</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">没错。前几天，找到我的手机时，我如释重负。我以为我把它弄丢了。这还是个新手机呢。找到它的时候，我超级开心。你呢，丹？</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: I ten<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> to sigh to show <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">frustration</strong>. And sometimes <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">resignation</strong>.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">沮丧时我会叹气。无奈的时候我也会叹气。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Catherine: Now, frustration is what we feel when thing<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s are</span></span>n't going well, when thing<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s are</span></span> annoyi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">ng us a</span></span>nd they don't work. When thing<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">s are</span></span> <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">frustrating</strong>.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">当某事进展不顺、困扰我们、不见成效或令人失望时，我们就会感到沮丧。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0.5em 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-top: 1px dashed rgb(206, 169, 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The moles came out just as you might see a mole come out in England. The dogs came out, barking the moment their heads were free, and struggling as you've seen them do when they are getting through a narrow hole in a hedge. The stags were the queerest to watch, for of course the antlers came up a long time before the rest of them, so at first Digory thought they were trees. The frogs, who all came up near the river, went straight into it with a plop-plop and a loud croaking. The panthers, leopards and things of that sort, sat down at once to wash the loose earth off their hind quarters and then stood up against the trees to sharpen their front claws.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">鼹鼠出来时与你在英国见的鼹鼠出洞一模一样。狗一伸出脑袋就汪汪地叫，像从篱笆的窄缝里钻过时那样挣扎着。雄鹿是最有趣的，因为它们的角比只他部分先出来很长时间，所以，一开始迪格雷以为是树。青蛙从河岸边钻出来后，就呱呱地叫着，一蹦一蹦地跳到河里去了。花豹、黑豹一类的动物马上坐下来，将后腿上沾的松土抖掉，然后站起身，在树上磨前爪。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:你好,我来登记入住。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">登记员:你一定是Larson先生吧。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:是的，没错。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">登记员:欢迎你住进天津国际大厦。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请你填一下这份登记表好吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;">旅客:好的。</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">登记员:谢谢你.......对不起，先生，你忘记填写签证号码了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">旅客:是吗？让我看看...... 喔，对不起...给你。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">登记员:先生,请你在这里签一下字，谢谢。您的房间号是2904，这是钥匙。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: Hi, I'm here to check in.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: You must be Mr. Larson.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: Yes, that's right.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Welcome to Tianjin International Building.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Would you please fill out this registration form?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: OK.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: Thank you ...Excuse me, sir. You forgot to fill in your visa number.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">G: Did I? Let me see that...Oh, sorry...Here you are.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">R: And would you sign here, please? Thank you. You're in room 2904. Here are your keys.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">His feeling has been harmed profoundly.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他的感情被_________伤害了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">深深地</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">研究小组认为，造成孤独感传播的原因是：孤独感会使人在对待他人时缺少肚量，更加消极。一旦一个人具有孤独感，他很有可能在和朋友进行交往时表现得很消极，而这些朋友也很可能会消极地影响他们的朋友。如果这种相互影响重复进行，朋友之间的关系就会变得紧张，人们就会变得更加孤独，更加自闭。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The reason for the spread, the team argues, is because loneliness causes people to act towards others in a less generous and more negative fashion. As someone becomes lonely, he is more likely to interact with his friends negatively, and they are then more likely to interact with other friends negatively. If these interactions are repeated, the ties of friendships fray and people become lonelier and more isolated.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", "Microsoft YaHei UI", "Microsoft YaHei", Arial, sans-serif;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-align: center;white-space: normal;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;'>9.29 每日一句：</strong><strong><span style="text-align: justify;">I have an idea.  </span></strong></p><p style="text-align: 使丰富，充实；强化；</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">rich adj. 富有的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">en- 动词前缀：使处于某种状态；使具有某种特性；</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">如 enlarge 使扩大；endanger 使危险</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Education can greatly <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">enrich</span></em></strong> your life.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: society.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">某些方面是，但它们也会<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">丰富</strong>我们的生活。</p></section><section 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># Subtitle</strong></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="display: style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;padding: 0px 25px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Are you okay? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Father. I'm -- I'm so glad you could come and pray for mama. Please, sit, sit. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Thank you, Gabrielle. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Listen, since you're here, there's something I've always wondered about. That whole thing about priests not being allowed to repeat what they hear in confessions is that a hard rule or just a general guide line? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Rest assured, everyone's secrets are safe. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's good to hear. I'll keep yours, too, if you want to talk. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Oh, me? No, no. Confession's not really my thing. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">That's a shame. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Okay, you can stop condemning me with your eyes. Right now. I know you know about the affair, but you know nothing about my life. Look, it's not even an issue anymore. John and I are finished. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Gabrielle, the church is pretty clear on this. If you commit a mortal sin and you die without repenting, you go to hell. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Well, aren't you just a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">ball of fun</strong>.</p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: right;font-size: 11px;line-height: 2;padding: 0px 25px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">滑动查看完整台词</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="font-size: 17px;color: rgb(43, 65, 110);letter-spacing: 2px;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># 有话说 #</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="justify-content: center;margin: 1px 0% 0px;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100px;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;border-top: 0px solid rgb(43, 65, 110);border-top-left-radius: 0px;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 8px;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(43, 65, 110);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -24px 0% 10px;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 46px;height: 33px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(244, 235, 229);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 206% 134% 167% 138%;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频，大家有没有发现我们要讲的“有趣的人”该如何在英语中去表达呢？没错，今天我们要来分享的就是“a ball of fun”～🤣 🤣 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 15px;height: 15px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 225, 139, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: -5px;width: 10px;height: 10px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 189, 218, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;padding-left: 6px;padding-right: 6px;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(121, 36, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a ball of fun</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);width: 10px;height: 10px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 189, 218, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: -5px;width: 15px;height: 15px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 225, 139, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们先来看一下a ball of <span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达，正常的英语表达中也会常常看到，就比如说一个雪球，一个毛线团 分别可以表达为“a ball of snow” 和 “a ball of wool”~ 这些都比较具象，那么“a ball of fun”就是抽象转具象的一种表达，形容“有趣的人”～ 这样理解就印象深刻了吧！🧐 🧐 </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a ball of fun</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太逗了／</strong>她就是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">开心果</strong>！</p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">再来一个抽象转具象的表达：</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: 139, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: -5px;width: 10px;height: 10px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 189, 218, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;padding-left: 6px;padding-right: 6px;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(121, 36,
