0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"># 有话说 #</strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="justify-content: center;margin: 1px 0% 0px;display: flex;flex-flow: row nowrap;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100px;vertical-align: top;flex: 0 0 auto;height: auto;border-top: 0px solid rgb(43, 65, 110);border-top-left-radius: 0px;align-self: flex-start;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0% 8px;justify-content: center;transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(1px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="background-color: rgb(43, 65, 110);height: 1px;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: -24px 0% 10px;justify-content: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 46px;height: 33px;vertical-align: top;overflow: hidden;background-color: rgb(244, 235, 229);border-width: 0px;border-radius: 206% 134% 167% 138%;border-style: none;border-color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">看完视频，大家有没有发现我们要讲的“有趣的人”该如何在英语中去表达呢？没错，今天我们要来分享的就是“a ball of fun”～🤣 🤣 </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;width: 15px;height: 15px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 225, 139, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: -5px;width: 10px;height: 10px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 189, 218, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;padding-left: 6px;padding-right: 6px;font-size: 16px;color: rgb(121, 36, 36);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a ball of fun</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);width: 10px;height: 10px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 189, 218, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: middle;margin-left: -5px;width: 15px;height: 15px;border-radius: 50%;background-color: rgba(255, 225, 139, 0.5);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们先来看一下a ball of <span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这个表达，正常的英语表达中也会常常看到，就比如说一个雪球，一个毛线团 分别可以表达为“a ball of snow” 和 “a ball of wool”~ 这些都比较具象，那么“a ball of fun”就是抽象转具象的一种表达，形容“有趣的人”～ 这样理解就印象深刻了吧！🧐 🧐 </span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She is <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">a ball of fun</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">她<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">太逗了／</strong>她就是个<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">开心果</strong>！</p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">再来一个抽象转具象的表达：</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please follow the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">general guideline</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请自觉遵守<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">规则</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">rest assured (that) ...</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">放心</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You may <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">rest assured</strong> that we'll make payment in time.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">请<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">放心</strong>，我们会按时付款的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You can <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">rest assured</strong> that we'll give you the morning call at 6: 00 am.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">您<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">放心</strong>，我们会在早上6点钟叫醒您的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">XX is not really my thing</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我是真不喜欢XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Durian <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">is not really my thing</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我不喜欢</strong>吃榴莲。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be clear on sth</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">对....一清二楚</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">I'm clear on</strong> what you have done.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">我对</strong>你做的事<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">一清二楚</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">commit a motal sin</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">犯下不可饶恕的大罪</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">motal sin 滔天大罪</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"></strong></p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 0.5em;margin-bottom: 0.5em;padding-left: 0.5em;padding-right: 0.5em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="box-sizing: border-box;width: 85%;border-width: 0.3em;border-style: solid;border-color: white;box-shadow: rgb(102, 102, 102) 0.2em 0.2em 0.5em;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;height: auto !important;"><img data-ratio="0.4509259" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/L4LJPfaSIKfjtGfiaxBJ8E70OvUabqUU6DZHl0nPTnOvUQ1qy7GbNVWmMNDjVUW6vx5n4w6yhTzTb6sNDdDgboA/640?wx_fmt=png" data-type="png" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 30px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="text-align: justify;line-height: 2;letter-spacing: 1px;padding: 0px 30px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Every person may <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">commit a motal sin</strong>, and he would only be forgiven by repenting of what he had done.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">世人都有可能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">犯下不可饶恕的罪过</strong>，并且只有忏悔自己的罪过才能被宽恕。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">今天的分享就到这里啦~</span></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 12px;box-sizing: border-box;">实用词链儿积累起来吧~</span></p><p style="text-align: center;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-bottom: 3px double rgb(218, 214, 205);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;box-sizing: data-type="png" data-w="300" style="vertical-align: middle;max-width: 100%;width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;" width="100%"/></section></section></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 30%;border-bottom: 3px double rgb(218, 214, 205);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfjtGfiaxBJ8E70OvUabqUU6d49hDQ4uI1YU5NwmHXnBsZAwIibT6jUwXXVXejiajYW9FNp9z0gJOGDg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="258" border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 80%;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 11px;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);line-height: 1.6;letter-spacing: 3px;padding: 0px 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="background-color: rgba(230, 154, 88, 0.26);box-sizing: border-box;"> TeacherGwen </span></p></section></section></section></section></section></sectio</section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.resignation  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˌrezɪɡˈneɪʃn  ; NAmE ˌrezɪɡˈneɪʃn  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">n.顺从；听任</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：patient willingness to accept a difficult or unpleasant situation that you cannot change</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'm not talking about resignation. What I'm talking about is active acceptance.我说的不是屈从 我说的是主动接受。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">They accepted their defeat with resignation. 他们无可奈何地承认失败。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She bore the pain with resignation.她默默地忍受着痛苦。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.resigned  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ rɪˈzaɪnd  ; NAmE rɪˈzaɪnd  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">adj.逆来顺受的；顺从的</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：being willing to calmly accept sth unpleasant or difficult that you cannot change</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">But they also seem resigned to the fact that they can't keep this from happening.但是看起来民众也接受了这样一个事实，即他们不能阻止这种事件的发生。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">" Most men lead lives of quiet desperation" . Don't be resigned to that. Break out.「大部分的人生活在平静的绝望中」别就此认命，而应该奋力突破。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.on average  平均；普通，通常</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We've saved on average about $3,000 a month.我们平均每个月节省了$3,000。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.reckon  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈrekən  ; NAmE ˈrekən  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.想；认为</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to think sth or have an opinion about sth</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I reckon (that) I'm going to get that job. 我认为我会得到那份工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">‘They'll never find out.’ ‘ You reckon?’ (= I think you may be wrong about that.) “他们永远不会发现。”“是吗？”</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5.regulate  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ ˈreɡjuleɪt  ; NAmE ˈreɡjuleɪt  /</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.调节，控制（速度、压力、温度等）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to control the speed, pressure, temperature, etc. in a machine or system</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">My watch is losing time; I will have to regulate it.我的表慢了，我必须调整它。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Take care to regulate the point of balance. Place it at your waist. 注意调节重心，保持在腰部。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6.defence mechanism  防御机制</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">When my parents got divorced is when I started using humour as a defence mechanism.我父母离婚后我开始用幽默来自我保护。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">7.cope  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ kəʊp  ; NAmE koʊp  / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">v.（成功地）对付，处理</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to deal successfully with sth difficult</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I got to the stage where I wasn't coping any more. 到了这个阶段，我已经无法应付了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He wasn't able to cope with the stresses and strains of the job. 对付这项工作的紧张与压力，他无能为力。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">8.switch off/on  关╱开（电灯、机器等）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英英释义：to turn a light, machine, etc. off/on by pressing a button or switch</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Please switch the lights off as you leave. 你离开的时候请把灯关了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">How do you switch this thing on? 这东西怎么开？</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: 1.15em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 6px;height: 6px;margin-top: -3px;border-radius: 100%;float: left;background-color: rgb(232, 181, 181);box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="border-top: 1px solid rgb(232, 181, 181);width: 99.9%;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="text-align: right;margin: -1.1em 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);text-align: left;padding: 3px 10px;color: rgb(249, I<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(2, 165, 227);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> sounds like we humans never sto<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(2, 165, 227);box-sizing: border-box;">p</span></span> sighing!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">解脱，无奈，沮丧，重置肺部活动。我们人类好像在不停地叹气。</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;">Dan: We<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(191, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">ll, a</span></span>ctually, we humans sigh on average 12 times an hour. ha<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(2, 165, 227);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span> reset. 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: thi<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(191, 0, 0);box-sizing: border-box;">s is a</span></span> little bi<span style="text-decoration: style="color: rgb(2, 165, 227);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span>. I<span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(2, 165, 227);box-sizing: border-box;">t</span></span> means to set – or choose - a new password.</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;box-sizing: border-box;">你可以重置密码，这和上面的重置有些不同。这是指设置或选择一个新密码。</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br 203);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Showers of birds came out of the trees. Bees got to work on the flowers as if they hadn't a second to lose. But the greatest moment of all was when the biggest hump broke like a small earthquake and out came the sloping back, the large, wise head, and the four baggy-trousered legs of an elephant. And now you could hardly hear the song of the Lion; there was so much cawing, cooing, crowing, braying, neighing, baying, barking, lowing, bleating, and trumpeting.      </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">林中传来阵阵鸟鸣。蜜蜂一秒钟也不愿耽误就在花上忙开了。但最壮观的时刻是当最大的圆丘像轻度地震一样炸裂开时，从里而隆起大象斜坡般的脊背、聪明的大脑袋和四条像穿着宽松裤子一般的大腿。现在，你几乎听不见狮子的歌唱了，四面八方，满耳的牛叫、马嘶、犬吠、鸟鸣…</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:我需要明天很早就到机场，你能提前为我安排一辆出租车吗？我怕6:00 的时候在街上找不到出租车。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B:当然。您想在明晨6:00的时候要一辆出租车吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:是的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 好的，我会为您安排一辆出租车，然后给您打电话请您确认一下。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A:非常感谢。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 您好，Konnor先生吗？这里是前台接待处。出租车将在明天早上6:00等着接您去机场。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 太好了，大约多少钱？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 去机场大约60元。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I need to go to the airport very early tomorrow morning. Could you arrange a taxi for me in advance? I'm afraid I won't be able to find one on the street at 6:00 in the morning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Certainly. So you'd like a taxi for 6:00 a.m.?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Yes.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Okay. I'll arrange a taxi for you, then call you to confirm it.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Thanks very much.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Hello, Mr. Konnor? This is Reception. A taxi will be waiting to take you to the airport at 6:00 tomorrow morning.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Great. And how much will it be?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: To the airport it should be about 60 yuan.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I won't listen to such vicious remarks.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我不想听这种_________话。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">恶毒的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">汉译英</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这种影响在朋友间比在家人之间更为明显，女人之间比男人之间更明显。研究者认为这是由于舍弃一段友情的代价要比舍弃一段亲情的代价小。并且，相较于男人，女人在情感和社会上求助于朋友的次数要多得多。一旦他们无法接受什么，就很可能变得孤独。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The effects were more noticeable among friends than family, and stronger among women than men. The researchers argue that this is because the costs of abandoning relationships are lower for friends than they are for family members, and because women look to friends for emotional and social support more than men do. When they fail to receive it, they are more likely to become lonely.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: center;"><strong style='max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Helvetica Neue", "PingFang SC", "Hiragino Sans GB", style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(151, 195, 123, 0.44);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="font-size: 15px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">Down by the riverside, I laid my burdens down, now I'm traveling light.</span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></strong></p></section></section></section></section></section></section></section></section><br/></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-5px, 0px, 0px);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 注意down中的元音滑动/a—ʊ/，尤其注意双元音中的第一个元音/a/的口型；</p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. burden中的/dn/音可发成鼻腔爆破，也可发成/dən/。无须刻意追求。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：down by the river/riverside 在河边</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">I found a lovely eatery <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">down by the river</span></strong></em>. </p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">在河边</strong>发现一间别致的小餐馆。</p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: data-type="jpeg" data-w="500" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: unset;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">2. 词链儿：lay down the burdens 放下重担</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">①放下→lay down</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">Daniel finished the article and </span><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">laid the newspaper down</span></em></strong></span><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> on his desk</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">丹尼尔看完文章后<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">把报纸放在</strong>他的书桌上。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">②规定→lay down</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">The Companies Act </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">lays down</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> a set of minimum requirements </span><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">《公司法》<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">规定</strong>了一系列最低标准。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">3. 词链儿：travel light 轻装前行</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">I will </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">travel light</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"> this time. </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">这次我要<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">少带东西去旅行</strong>。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">He likes to </span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">travel light</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">. </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">他喜欢<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">轻装旅行</strong>。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: border-box;">travel light</span></em></strong><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">.  </span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">有经验的旅行者<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">旅行时带很少东西</strong>。</span></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;box-sizing: style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. ta<span style="color: rgb(95, 156, 239);text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;">ke</span> c<span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">are(r) o</span>f  相同的/k/音相遇，舍前留后；</strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. close</strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">作形容词时，尾音为 /s/</strong></p><p style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">作动词时，尾音为/z/。</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">本句来自 Mother Teresa 特蕾莎修女</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.4704641" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfgSMBYHoS4rJibRiauPCkyxnicpersGKr4cK63cEKnmHzsWmn65grUJhKfsMicJsWkwZOKqwEl7qzia9A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="474" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. 词链儿：take care of XX 照顾XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">Please <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">take care of </span></strong></em>my child while I am away. </p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">我离开时，请<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">照料</strong>我的孩子。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">Take care! 保重！</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">拓展：（委婉表示）收拾某人、揍某人</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">I'll <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">take care </span></em></strong><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">of</span></em></strong> you later. </p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">等会我再<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">收拾</strong>你（的事儿）！</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. close</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">①作动词 <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">关闭</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">Close</span></em></strong> the door. <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关上</strong>门。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.562963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfgSMBYHoS4rJibRiauPCkyxn6G2rkegehrYZzXIu8UfLPiaWvtVlbg5S1hiaAlyGq60ObjHCNXzsupag/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">②作形容词 <span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">亲近</span></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">We were very <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">close</span></em></strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"> 我们<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">关系很好</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">To the Italian people, that's a very sacred, <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">close</span></em></strong> relationship. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">对意大利人而言，那是一种神圣的、<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">亲密的</strong>关系。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;box-sizing: border-box;"><img data-ratio="0.562963" data-src="https://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/L4LJPfaSIKfgSMBYHoS4rJibRiauPCkyxnf85V7qlH0VTxAkCfatNtnUEaW9a47qFPjgUZtrfM2qBAu5411tuhibw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg" data-type="jpeg" data-w="1080" style="vertical-align: middle;box-sizing: border-box;"/></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="text-align: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">*close的用法：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be close to somebody 与XX关系亲密</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">be close to doing something 接近XX</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">He gotta <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">be close to</span></em></strong> finishing by now.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">他现在<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">差不多</strong>也该结束了。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">He wanted to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">be close to</span></em></strong> the people.</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">他很想<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">接近</strong>这些人们。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">You're the <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">closest</span></em></strong> thing I ever had to a brother. <br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">你是我所拥有过的，最<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">接近于</strong>亲兄弟的人了。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">...if you would ever <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span
